| <span data-ttu-id="b0fe1-689">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b0fe1-689">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="b0fe1-690">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b0fe1-690">Value</span></span> |
